# GitHub activity 2021 December 24th

**The** `GitHub stars & follow` **file is receiving an expansion. Starting February 26th 2021, I am now keeping a log of all activities.**

**Note:** forked repositories are starred by default, unless I say otherwise (3 examples from 1 repo: [Why-you-should-stop-using-Google-analytics](https://github.com/seanpm2001/Why-you-should-stop-using-Google-analytics) along with some other projects)

### Unfollows

After further review and under a new emergency protocol, I have unfollowed 2 users due to malicious activity, promotion of propaganda, and extremely spammy bot-like behavior. This incident will be reported. - July 11th 2021

#### July 11th 2021

1. [https://github.com/cxk-bugsfly](https://github.com/cxk-bugsfly/)

2. [https://github.com/Sherlockcxk](https://github.com/Sherlockcxk/)

#### July 26th 2021

A 3rd bot account has been identified:

3. [https://github.com/CXK-53](https://github.com/CXK-53/)

This is the 3rd account to duplicate the first 2 accounts. There seems to be some manipulation of the Algorithm by swapping their location for these accounts between California and China. They are also using the code ```CXK``` and as of July 26th 2021, have farmed over 300 stars on 1 project known as Rickroll-lang. They are using this message to gain attention:

```
Star my repo “Rick-Lang/rickroll-lang", and I will star all of your pinned repos!
```

Please report these bots if they are still going as of reading this. These are not genuine stars you are gaining if you are still wanting to participate in this.

#### 2021 September 6th

A 4th account followed me (I can tell it was one of the CXK accounts, as it had the same description), and I relented. I have failed.

[https://github.com/XuQingGen/](https://github.com/XuQingGen/)

This might not hold, if change doesn't occur soon, I will unfollow again. I feel like I deserved to lose 4 followers the next day for this.

# Organizations to follow (when organizations become followable)

## GitHub

https://github.com/education

https://github.com/cli/ { GitHubs command line tool }

https://github.com/github/ { GitHub, where people build software }

## Microsoft

https://github.com/microsoft { Microsoft [::] }

https://github.com/MicrosoftDocs { Microsoft Documentation }

https://github.com/MicrosoftLearning { Microsoft Machine Learning }

https://github.com/microsoftgraph { Unified endpoint for accessing data, relationships and insights coming from the Microsoft cloud }

https://github.com/Azure { Microsoft Azure }

## Linux

`No organization found :(`

## Mozilla

https://github.com/mozilla/ { Mozilla foundation }

## Apple

https://github.com/apple {Apple Inc} { MacOS 12, iOS 15, iPadOS 15, support coming soon }

## VideoLan

https://github.com/videolan { VLC Media Player }

## KDE

https://github.com/KDE { K Desktop Environment }

## Other

https://github.com/lincity-ng/ { City simulator game for Linux }

https://github.com/ruffle-rs { Flash player emulator written in Rust }

https://github.com/GNOME { GNOME Desktop Environment/GNOME Software project, other than the desktop environment }

https://github.com/IBM { International Business Computers }

https://github.com/dell { Thank you for supporting Linux }

https://github.com/canonical { Creators of Ubuntu }

https://github.com/pocketgems { Legacy mobile game producer that made some of the games from my childhood time on iOS 5 and 6 }

https://github.com/dlang { Programming language }

https://github.com/lfe { Programming language }

https://github.com/rebol { Programming language }

https://github.com/cappuccino { Objective-J framework }

https://github.com/apache { Apache Software foundation }

https://github.com/crystal-lang/ { Programming language }

https://github.com/Shopify { Creators of the Liquid programming language }

https://github.com/qemu { Creators of the Qemu emulator }

https://github.com/WinWorldPC { Creators of the WinWorldPC archive website }

https://github.com/dogecoin { Very wow, much doge, such currency  }

https://github.com/bitcoin { Cries in BitCoin value dropping }

https://github.com/TryItOnline { For various online IDEs for executing code online }

https://github.com/racket { Programming language }

https://github.com/NixOS { For NixOS and the Nix package manager }

https://github.com/the-yoom-project { An experiment for a SB2/SB3-based browser, Scratch 2/3 }

https://github.com/dracula { Specialized dark theme for various programs }

https://github.com/haskell { Programming language }

# Alt account

This is the data for my GitHub alt account, [seanwallawalla](https://github.com/seanwallawalla) this account is used for testing, debugging, and promotion. It does not contain any projects, is not part of an organization, and is not actively used.

This section was created on March 11th 2021, when I wanted to use the account.
